 aropiyon ke khilaaf bhartiya dand samhita (ipisi) kii dhara 419 (praturupan kar dhokhadhadi), dhokhadhadi (420), jaalsaji (467), dhokhadhadi ke uddeshy se jaalsaji (468, 471) farji dastavej ko asli kii tarah istemaal karnaa (474) or aapraadhik shadyantr (120 bi) ke tahat maamla darj kiya gaye he
 At the same time, eight people have been accused in the Pre PG Test 2011 case
 in aropiyon ke khilaaf dhara 419, 420, 467, 468, 471 or 120bi ke tahat maamla darj kiya gaya he
 According to the CBI, a case has been registered against 21 people in the Pre Medical Test (PMT-2010) case
 aropiyon ke khilaaf dhara 419, 420, 467, 468, 471, 474 or 120bi ke tahat prakaran darj kiye gaye hai
 The second case was registered in the Pre PG Test-2011 case, in which eight people have been made accused
 in aropiyon ke khilaaf dhara 419, 420, 467, 468, 471 or 120bi ke tahat prakaran darj kiye gaye hai
 a case of Madhya Pradesh Accredited Examination Act has also been filed on the accused of prepg examination
 yah donon prakaran sibiai jaanch ke pramukh sanyukt nideshak aar

 is maamle main kul 28 logon ko aaropee banaaya gaya he

 paanchavi praathmiki main nijee chikitsa mahavidhyalayon main piemti-2011 seat aavanton maamle main darj kii gai he, jisamen teen logon ko aaropee banaaya gaya he

 sibiai ab tak jaanch kar rahi estf or jile str par gathit police kii esaiti ke saath kai daur kii baithken kar chuki he

 sutron ke anusaar abhi tak jaanch kar rahi estf ne vyaapman ghotaale main kul 55 prakaran darj kiye gaye the

 is jaanch ke dauraan 48 logon kii maut ho chuki he

 Dinesh Karthik's 33-ball 69 helped Kings XI Punjab maintain their hopes of reaching the playoffs by defeating Kochi Tuskers Kerala by six wickets in the crucial IPL match
 captain mahela jayavardhane ke 76 ran ke dam par kochi taskars kerala ne saat wicket par 178 ran banaae
 In reply, Punjab had a poor start and their two wickets in the fifth over were up for 31 but Karthik and Shaun Marsh (42) added 111 runs for the third wicket to take the team out of trouble
 priti jinta kii team ne jeet kaa lakshya saat gend shesh rahete hasil kar liya
 Karthik scored 69 runs in 33 balls with the help of seven fours and five sixes
 marsh ne unka bakhubi saath dete hue 30 gend main 42 ran banaae jisamen paanch chauke or do chakke shaamil the
 With this win, Punjab has moved up to sixth place in the table with 10 points from 11 matches while Kochi is at seventh position with 10 points from 12 matches
 kochi ke gharelu maidan holkar stadium par ipel kaa yah pehla match tha
 Kochi got off to a great start when sent for batting first
 brendan maikulam (32) ke saath pari kii shuruyaat karne vaale jayavardhane ne 52 gend kaa saamana karke aath chauke or do chakke lagaae
 Jayawardene and mccullum scored just 8
 4 over main 93 ran jod liye
 National Award-winning actress Shweta Basu, who was caught on charges of prostitution in Hyderabad, told the police that she came into the business due to lack of films and lack of money
 kaary bal ke adhikariyon ne 31 agast ko banjaaraa hills ilaake ke ek hotel main chhapemari kar ek deh vyapaar giroh kaa bhandaphod kiya tha
 The gang included actress Shweta Basu, who won the National Film Award for Best Child Artist for the film 'spider' in 2002
 vah film 'ikbaal' main bhi najar ai thim
 Apart from this, Shweta also acted in 'wow Life Ho To Aisi' and 'darna Necessary'
 vah ekta kapur ke lokapriy serial 'kahani ghar-ghar kii' main bhi bal kalakaar ke rup main kaam kar chuki thi
 Balu, assistant director of Tollywood, who worked as an agent for the actress, was arrested
 atirikt police upayukta en koti reddy ne aaj kaha ki poochtacha ke dauraan abhinetri ne kaha ki filmein na milane or paison kii kami hone se vah deh vyapaar main ai
 Reddy said, the actress is a victim, she has not been arrested
 use ek bachaav grih main bheja gaya he, jabaki baaluu ko aniatik taskari rokthaam adhinium ke tahat giraftaar kiya gaya
 The hearing in the Supreme Court on the ownership of the disputed land has been postponed till January 2019 amid the ongoing political debate in the country regarding the construction of the Ram temple in Ayodhya
 isse pehle is maamle main sarvocch nyaayalay main sunwaayee karte hue 1994 ke ismail faruki vanam bhartiya sangh maamle main apane faisle ko purnvichaar ke liye badi bench ko bhejne se inkaar karte hue kaha tha ki ismail faruki cese main adaalat kii tippanee sirf bhoomi adhigrahan sambandhi maamalon main lagu hogi or is faisle kaa ram janmabhumi vivaad ke maamle main koi prabhaav nahin padegaa
 On Monday, a three-member bench of Chief Justice of Supreme Court Ranjan Gogoi, Justice SK Kaul and Justice KM Joseph has fixed January 2019 as the date of the case
 sarvocch nyaayalay main yah sunwaayee 2010 ke elahabadaaai courtke faisle ke khilaaf daayar punarvichaar yachikaaon par honi he
 What was the Allahabad High Court's decision? On September 30, 2010, the Lucknow bench of the Allahabad High Court gave a historic verdict on Ayodhyamale
 justise sudhir agarwal, justise es you khan or justise di ve sharma kii bench ne faisle main 2
 The disputed land of 77 acres was divided into three equal parts
 jisamen ram lalaa virajman vaala hissaa hindu mahasabha ko diya gaya
 The second part was given to the Nirmohi Akhara and the third part to the Sunni Waqf Board

 1

 2
 bharat ke sansad kaa golakaar dikhnaa uske kabhi na thaharne kaa pratik he

 3
 The Library within the Parliament is the second largest library in the country
 4
 The shape of the Lok Sabha and the Rajya Sabha is similar to a horseshoe
 5
 During this inflation, you can get one person's food for 12 rupees in Parliament canteen
 6
 The carpet inside the Lok Sabha is green
 yah bharat kekrishi samruddhika pratik he
 The carpet of the Rajya Sabha of India is red in color

 7
 bharat ke raashtrapati kaa offis 13 number he

 8
 The first hour (11 to 12) of the proceedings of the House is called the Question Hour
 is dauransaansad policy, sarkaar ke kaam or alag-alag bilon par charchaa karte hai
 9
 12 baje saansad lok sabha adhyaksh ko suchit kar kisi bhimahatvapurn muddaper bahes kar sakate hai
 This is called zero time
 10
 Money bills are passed only through Lok Sabha
 lok sabha main paas kiye jane ke baad kisi pherbadal ke liye rajya sabha main bheja jaataa he
 It does not pass from Rajya Sabha
 11
 In case of emergency, the President can extend the Lok Sabha for one year

 Finland company HMD Global recently launched Nokia 7 Plus in India
 bharat sahit duniya bhar main ek samay main nokia ke mobile phone kaaphi popular the
 But now only Nokia's smartphones will not be able to do wonders, because at one time they were popular
 iske liye company ko phir ke khud ko sabit karnaa hoga, or yahi vajah he ki nokia ke nae smartfones lagaataar bazaar main aa rahe hai
 One of them is Nokia 7 Plus and we have reviewed it
 jaanane kii koshish kii he, kya yah smartphone company ke daawey par khara utarataa he
 In this review you will read: Design / Build Quality - Where does Nokia 7 Plus stand in design and build quality
 disple or parformens – kya behtareen hardware ise asal jindagi main powerful banaate hai?yujar experience – kya ise yuj karke aapako nokia mobile kii feel aati he? kya ise yuj karnaa acha anubhav hecamera or bydaree – photography main kya kamaal dikhaa paaya yah smartphone ye bataaenge, saath hi bydaree kab tak aapkaa saath de sakati he is rivyuu main aapako yah bhi pataa chalegaa
 Full review design and build quality - you will experience a premium device as soon as you hold it, at the same time you will understand that this smartphone is durable
 aisa isliye kyonki company ne isamen 6000 siries aluminium block yuj kiya he jise durable hone ke liye janaa jaataa he
 We have reviewed the black copper variant
 Nokia 7 Plus kaa dizin behtareen he iske aij par copper diya gaya he or blike ke saath yah shandaar lagata he
 The camera and fingerprint scanner have a copper finish which makes it look even better
 nokia kii branding peeche kii taraf he
 There is a vertical dual camera setup in the rear and a fingerprint scanner is given below it
 camera ke bagal main dual elidi flash diya gaya he
 Underneath the phone is the branding of Android One
 wolum rocker or lock kies dayee taraf hai jabaki baayin taraf aapako sim, memri card trey miltaa he
 There is a USB Type c jack at the bottom with a speaker grill and a headphone jack at the top
 displacenok 7 Plus main 6 inch kii phul echdi plus disple di gai he or aspect reshyo 18:9 kaa he
 The display is resolution (2160X1440) and IPS LCD panel is used and Gorilla Glass 3 is given above
 disple pehali najar main brit lagati he or yuj ke saath aapaki ankhon ko pareshaan nahin karti he
 Viewing angle is also good
 There is no problem in viewing the display from any corner
 disple badi he or ise videos dekhnaa ek acha anubhav he or gaming main bhi disple kaa parformens behtareen he
 But you may have some difficulty in viewing the content of the display in the sunlight
 dabl tap vedap jaise kuch fitures bhi hai jisase disple yuses main aapako aasaani hoti he
 Performance This smartphone has 4GB RAM with Qualcomm Snapdragon 660 processor
 internal memory 64GB he jise micro esady card ke jariye 256GB tak badhaayaa ja saktaa he
 You may have a different opinion about the processor here, as Snapdragon 835 processor smartphones are also available in this range
 lekin company ne ise behatar tareeke se customij kiya he jisase behatar yujar experience miltaa he
 Although Snapdragon 835 would have been given, it would certainly have been much better
 bahraal hamane ise lagaataar yuj kiya he or is aadhaar par kah sakate hai ki yah smartphone lag nahin karata
 Gaming for a long time makes this phone hot
 haalanki gaming ke dauraan kai apl becoground main chal rahe hon to bhi hang nahin hota, na hi gaming main koi pareshaani hoti he
 This smartphone heats up even if you continue watching videos
 ap switch karnaa yani ek ap se duusare ap main janaa aasaan he, loding time kam he or aapako pataa nahin chalata he
 But if you are a power user and are using many heavy apps simultaneously, then there may be a problem for you
 Android One is smartphone ke yujar experience ko behatar banaata he
 It has little blotware and is pure Android
 security ptch milte rahete hai or company ne ise android van ke saath achche se customij kiya he
 If you want to use many more launchers or custom skin here, then there can be problems and there may be a problem of phone hang
 overol parformens aivarej se behatar kahi ja sakati he
 Dual rear camera setup has been given in the Camarais smartphone
 inamen ek lens 12 megapixl kaa he jiskaa aparchar f / 1
 Is 7
 doosraa lens 13 megapixl kaa he or yah telephoto he
 The specialty of these Nokia smartphones is the Bothi feature which is much better for content creators and journalists
 Nokia 7 Plus kaa rier or front camera ekh saath camera kaam karata he yani aap front or rier camere kaa istemaal ek baar main hi kar sakate hai
 This becomes a very important feature when you have to record someone's interview and you do not have any camera person
 hamane ise yuj kiya he yah behtareen he
 Other companies should also give such a feature now
 camera main optical image stebligeshan (OIS) nahin he or isaki kami hamen photography ke dauraan khali he
 For photography we found this smartphone average, because in daylight it can click good pictures, but low light and indoor clicked pictures can disappoint you
 becoground bler jis tarah se hona chahie, zyaadaatar baar nahin hota or yah ajeeb lagata he
 The company has given ZEISS optics in it, from which we had high expectations
 selfi camera 16 megapixl kaa he or selfi behtareen clic kar sakate hai
 The quality of the picture is also good
 2X juum karke clic kii gayi tasviren bhi acchhee hai, isamen koi pareshaani nahin he
 Overall camera performance is good, but it could have been improved further
 bydareebydaree ke maamle main nishchit taur par yah smartphone behtareen he
 The company has a 3,800mah battery in this smartphone
 ek baar phul charge karke aap puure din ise aaraam se chalaa sakate hai
 During this time you can do web browsing, social media, music and calling by keeping the internet on, which is usually done by a normal smartphone user
 fast charging saport hone kii vajah se yah jaldi charge hota he or isaki standbai timming bhi niraash nahin karti
 If you leave the smartphone without using it, it will be on for a few days
 overol bydaree parformens shandaar he or acchhee bydaree vaala behtareen smartphone kharidne kii soch rahe hai to yah jaahir he aapke liye hi he
 Price - Rs 25,990 (e-commerce websites)
 Should you take this smartphone? You are a fan of Nokia, liked the Bothy feature, want a durable phone or want a long battery life, then you can buy this phone
 iske alaava letest android / security chahie to bhi yah phone aapke liye he
 If you are fond of photography, this smartphone is not for you if you are a power user
